<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изречь.html>изре́чь</a> (10345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-речь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-rečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изречь.html>изре́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izréčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изрекать.html>изрека́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to utter, to speak solemnly / pompously
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изречь.html>изре́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрый.html>му́дрое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izréčʹ</b> múdroje slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to utter a word of wisdom</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mouth, to say</li></ol>

***изрешетить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изрешетить.html>изрешети́ть</a> (26493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">решети́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изрешетить.html>изрешети́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izrešetítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">решети́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изреше́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover completely in holes, to pierce in many places, to riddle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изрешетить.html>изрешети́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуля.html>пу́лями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>izrešetílo</b> púljami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was <b>riddled</b> with bullets</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решетка.html>решётка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rešótka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">решёточка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rešótočka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решетчатый.html>реше́тчатый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rešétčatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***изрыгать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́ть</a> (22339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изры́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izrýgnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izrygátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изры́гнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to belch, to disgorge, to spew out
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  Александр Суханов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Sukhanov" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Sukhanov">Alexander Sukhanov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>Драко́н</a></cite>  | <cite>Dragon playing the violin</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Моя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>дорога́я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́я</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>драко́н</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́н</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I skazál on: Moja dorogája, ne mogú ja, ogónʹ <b>izrygája</b>, v bášne žitʹ kak drakón, što za glúpyj zakón...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And he said: My dear, as I belch fire, I cannot live in a tower, what a silly regulation...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изувечить.html>изуве́чить</a> (16467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уве́чить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvéčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изувечить.html>изуве́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izuvéčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уве́чить</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изуве́чивать</b>)

***изумительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изумительный.html>изуми́тельный</a> (11224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izumítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумительный.html>изуми́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izumítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изуми́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изуми́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>amazing, stupendous, wonderful</li></ol>

***изумить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a> (26737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izumítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумлять.html>изумля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to amaze, to astound, to astonish, to strike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to fill with surprise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изумление.html>изумле́ние</a> (4010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izumítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>amazement, astonishment, awe</li></ol>

***изуродовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изуродовать.html>изуро́довать</a> (8781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродовать.html>уро́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uródovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изуродовать.html>изуро́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izuródovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродовать.html>уро́довать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disfigure, to deform, to mar</li>
<li>to mutilate, to maim, to cripple</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урод.html>уро́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uród</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродливый.html>уро́дливый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uródlivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***изучать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучать.html>изуча́ть</a> (2487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучить.html>изучи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучать.html>изуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучить.html>изучи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to study, to learn <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">implying that an individual or a group is studying or learning something with an in-depth approach</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to familiarize oneself with, to master</li>
<li>to scrutinize</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучение.html>изуче́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izučénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
